id="articleContentWrapper"></div></div></div></main><script>        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {            const generateBtn = document.getElementById('generateBtn');            const copyBtn = document.getElementById('copyBtn');            const downloadBtn = document.getElementById('downloadBtn');            const saveToPhotosBtn = document.getElementById('saveToPhotosBtn');            const shareBtn = document.getElementById('shareBtn');            const articleContentWrapper = document.getElementById('articleContentWrapper');            const messageBox = document.getElementById('messageBox');            const columnCountInput = document.getElementById('columnCountInput');            const fontSelector = document.getElementById('fontSelector');            const articlePreviewSection = document.getElementById('articlePreviewSection');            const newspaperOutput = document.getElementById('newspaperOutput');            const toggleResizeBtn = document.getElementById('toggleResizeBtn');            const resizeHandles = document.querySelectorAll('.resize-handle');                        const hardcodedLogoUrl = "https://athawadavishesh.com/logo.webp";            const hardcodedNewspaperTitle = "आठवडा विशेष - डिजिटल";            let dynamicWebsiteUrl = '';            let fetchedTitle = 'मथळा';            let fetchedContent = 'येथे मजकूर लिहा...';            let featuredImage = null;            let featuredImageCaption = '';            let isResizable = false;            // Words to be removed from the article content            const wordsToRemove = [                'Edit Post',                'Copy URL',                'Follow Us',                'Facebook Share',                'Facebook',                'X',                'Print',                'Share',                'WhatsApp',                'Telegram'            ];            function showMessage(t, e = 'info') {                messageBox.textContent = t;                messageBox.classList.remove('hidden');                messageBox.classList.remove('bg-green-100', 'text-green-700', 'bg-red-100', 'text-red-700', 'bg-blue-100', 'text-blue-700');                if (e === 'success') {                    messageBox.classList.add('bg-green-100', 'text-green-700');                } else if (e === 'error') {                    messageBox.classList.add('bg-red-100', 'text-red-700');                } else if (e === 'info') {                    messageBox.classList.add('bg-blue-100', 'text-blue-700');                }            }            function hideMessage() {                messageBox.classList.add('hidden');            }            function dataURLtoBlob(t) {                const e = t.split(',')[0].match(/:(.*?);/)[1],                    a = atob(t.split(',')[1]),                    o = a.length,                    n = new Uint8Array(o);                for (let r = 0; r < o; r++) n[r] = a.charCodeAt(r);                return new Blob([n], { type: e });            }            function generateArticle(t, e, imageObj, columnCount, baseUrl, postId) {                const a = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10);                                let imageHtml = '';                if (imageObj && imageObj.url) {                    imageHtml = `                        <div class="article-image-wrapper"><img src="${imageObj.url}" alt="${imageObj.caption || 'Featured image'}" class="article-image" crossorigin="anonymous">                            ${imageObj.caption ? `<p class="image-caption">${imageObj.caption}</p>` : ''}                        </div>                    `;                }                const n = e.split('\n').map(t => {                    const e = t.trim();                    return e.length > 0 ? `<p>${e}</p>` : '';                }).join('');                const urlSection = postId                    ? `<a href="https://${baseUrl}/${postId}" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="text-blue-600 underline">${dynamicWebsiteUrl}</a>`                    : `<p>${dynamicWebsiteUrl}</p>`;                                const r = `                    <div class="flex justify-between items-center mb-4 flex-wrap"><div class="flex-1 min-w-[150px] mb-4 md:mb-0"><img src="${hardcodedLogoUrl}" alt="Newspaper Logo" class="h-16 w-auto max-w-[200px]" crossorigin="anonymous"></div><div class="text-right flex-1 min-w-[200px]"><h2 class="text-2xl font-bold">${hardcodedNewspaperTitle}</h2><p class="text-sm text-gray-500">${new Intl.DateTimeFormat('mr-IN', { dateStyle: 'full' }).format(new Date(a))}</p></div></div><div class="mb-2"><h1 class="text-5xl article-title-font text-center"><div class="pb-4">${t}</div><div class="h-1 w-full bg-black my-4"></div></h1></div><div id="article-content" class="article-content-container text-base leading-relaxed" style="--column-count: ${columnCount};">                        ${imageHtml}                        ${n}                    </div><div class="absolute bottom-4 left-0 right-0 text-center text-xs text-gray-600">                        ${urlSection}                    </div>                `;                articleContentWrapper.innerHTML = r;                articlePreviewSection.classList.remove('hidden');                copyBtn.classList.remove('hidden');                downloadBtn.classList.remove('hidden');                saveToPhotosBtn.classList.remove('hidden');                shareBtn.classList.add('hidden'); // Hide share button until download/copy is complete            }            const fetchArticleContent = () => {                showMessage('Generating article...', 'info');                                const base_url = window.location.hostname;                let post_id = null;                const url = window.location.href;                const matches = url.match(/p=(\d+)|archives\/(\d+)|(\d+)\/$/);                if (matches) {                    post_id = matches[1] || matches[2] || matches[3];                }                if (post_id) {                    dynamicWebsiteUrl = `Post ID: ${post_id} | ${base_url}`;                } else {                    dynamicWebsiteUrl = base_url;                }                                const titleElement = document.querySelector('h1.entry-title, .single-post-title, .post-title, .post-header h1');                if (titleElement) {                    fetchedTitle = titleElement.innerText.trim();                }                const contentElement = document.querySelector('div.entry-content, article.post-content, div.post-body');                if (contentElement) {                    let content = contentElement.innerText.trim();                    wordsToRemove.forEach(word => {                        content = content.replace(new RegExp(word, 'g'), '');                    });                                        if (titleElement && content.startsWith(titleElement.innerText.trim())) {                        content = content.substring(titleElement.innerText.trim().length).trim();                    }                    fetchedContent = content;                }                const imageElement = document.querySelector('img.wp-post-image, .post-thumbnail img, .entry-content img');                if (imageElement) {                    featuredImage = imageElement.src;                    const captionElement = imageElement.closest('figure')?.querySelector('figcaption') || imageElement.closest('.wp-caption')?.querySelector('.wp-caption-text');                    if (captionElement) {                        featuredImageCaption = captionElement.innerText.trim();                    }                }                                if (fetchedTitle && fetchedContent) {                    showMessage(`Successfully fetched content from the current article!`, 'success');                } else {                    showMessage(`Could not find content to fetch from the current article.`, "info");                }                                generateArticle(fetchedTitle, fetchedContent, { url: featuredImage, caption: featuredImageCaption }, columnCountInput.value, base_url, post_id);            };            const handleDownload = (isSaveToPhotos = false) => {                showMessage('Preparing image for download...', 'info');                const elementToCapture = document.getElementById('newspaperOutput');                html2canvas(elementToCapture, { scale: 2, useCORS: true }).then(canvas => {                     const dataUrl = canvas.toDataURL("image/jpeg");                    const a = document.createElement('a');                    a.download = 'newspaper_article.jpg';                    a.href = dataUrl;                    a.click();                    showMessage('Download complete!', 'success');                    shareBtn.classList.remove('hidden');                }).catch(t => {                    console.error('Download failed:', t);                    showMessage('Download failed. Please try again.', 'error');                });            };            generateBtn.addEventListener('click', fetchArticleContent);            copyBtn.addEventListener('click', async () => {                showMessage('Copying image to clipboard...', 'info');                try {                    const elementToCapture = document.getElementById('newspaperOutput');                    const canvas = await html2canvas(elementToCapture, { scale: 2, useCORS: true });                    const dataUrl = canvas.toDataURL("image/jpeg");                    const file = dataURLtoBlob(dataUrl);                                        if (navigator.clipboard && navigator.clipboard.write) {                        try {                            await navigator.clipboard.write([                                new ClipboardItem({ 'image/jpeg': file })                            ]);                            showMessage('Image copied to clipboard!', 'success');                            shareBtn.classList.remove('hidden');                        } catch (err) {                            console.error('Clipboard API write failed:', err);                            throw new Error('Fallback to manual copy');                        }                    } else {                        throw new Error('Fallback to manual copy');                    }                } catch (err) {                    console.error('Copy to clipboard failed:', err);                    if (err.message === 'Fallback to manual copy') {                        // Fallback using execCommand for older browsers or if modern API fails                        const img = document.createElement('img');                        img.src = document.getElementById('newspaperOutput').querySelector('canvas').toDataURL('image/jpeg');                        img.style.position = 'absolute';                        img.style.left = '-9999px';                        document.body.appendChild(img);                                                const range = document.createRange();                        range.selectNode(img);                        const selection = window.getSelection();                        selection.removeAllRanges();                        selection.addRange(range);                                                try {                            document.execCommand('copy');                            showMessage('Image copied to clipboard!', 'success');                            shareBtn.classList.remove('hidden');                        } catch (execErr) {                            console.error('execCommand failed:', execErr);                            showMessage('Copy failed. Please click "Download as JPG" and copy from your file manager.', 'error');                        } finally {                            document.body.removeChild(img);                        }                    } else {                            showMessage('Copy failed. Please click "Download as JPG" and copy from your file manager.', 'error');                    }                }            });                        downloadBtn.addEventListener('click', () => handleDownload());            saveToPhotosBtn.addEventListener('click', () => handleDownload(true));            shareBtn.addEventListener('click', async () => {                showMessage('Preparing image for sharing...', 'info');                try {                    const elementToCapture = document.getElementById('newspaperOutput');                    const canvas = await html2canvas(elementToCapture, { scale: 2, useCORS: true });                    const dataUrl = canvas.toDataURL("image/jpeg");                    const file = dataURLtoBlob(dataUrl);                    const filesArray = [                        new File([file], 'newspaper_article.jpg', { type: file.type })                    ];                    if (navigator.canShare && navigator.canShare({ files: filesArray })) {                        await navigator.share({                            files: filesArray,                            title: 'Marathi News Article',                            text: 'मी हा वर्तमानपत्र लेख तयार केला आहे. तो नक्की पहा!',                        });                    } else {                        // Fallback for browsers that don't support the API                        throw new Error('Web Share API not supported or sharing of files is not permitted.');                    }                    showMessage('Share successful!', 'success');                } catch (error) {                    // This catch block handles the 'user denied' permission and unsupported devices                    console.error('Share failed:', error);                    showMessage('Share failed. Please click "Download as JPG" and share the file manually.', 'error');                    downloadBtn.classList.remove('hidden');                }            });            fontSelector.addEventListener('change', (t) => {                document.body.style.fontFamily = t.target.value;            });                        columnCountInput.addEventListener('change', () => {                const base_url = window.location.hostname;                let post_id = null;                const url = window.location.href;                const matches = url.match(/p=(\d+)|archives\/(\d+)|(\d+)\/$/);                if (matches) {                    post_id = matches[1] || matches[2] || matches[3];                }                generateArticle(fetchedTitle, fetchedContent, { url: featuredImage, caption: featuredImageCaption }, columnCountInput.value, base_url, post_id);            });            toggleResizeBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {                isResizable = !isResizable;                if (isResizable) {                    newspaperOutput.classList.remove('fixed-size');                    newspaperOutput.classList.add('resizable');                    resizeHandles.forEach(handle => handle.classList.remove('hidden'));                } else {                    newspaperOutput.classList.remove('resizable');                    newspaperOutput.classList.add('fixed-size');                    resizeHandles.forEach(handle => handle.classList.add('hidden'));                }                const base_url = window.location.hostname;                let post_id = null;                const url = window.location.href;                const matches = url.match(/p=(\d+)|archives\/(\d+)|(\d+)\/$/);                if (matches) {                    post_id = matches[1] || matches[2] || matches[3];                }                generateArticle(fetchedTitle, fetchedContent, { url: featuredImage, caption: featuredImageCaption }, columnCountInput.value, base_url, post_id);            });            let activeHandle = null;            let initialX, initialY, initialWidth, initialHeight;            const onStart = (e) => {                e.preventDefault();                activeHandle = e.target;                const event = e.touches ? e.touches[0] : e;                initialX = event.clientX;                initialY = event.clientY;                initialWidth = newspaperOutput.offsetWidth;                initialHeight = newspaperOutput.offsetHeight;                                window.addEventListener('mousemove', onMove);                window.addEventListener('mouseup', onEnd);                window.addEventListener('touchmove', onMove);                window.addEventListener('touchend', onEnd);            };            const onMove = (e) => {                if (!activeHandle) return;                const event = e.touches ? e.touches[0] : e;                const dx = event.clientX - initialX;                const dy = event.clientY - initialY;                let newWidth, newHeight;                const rect = newspaperOutput.getBoundingClientRect();                if (activeHandle.classList.contains('bottom-right')) {                    newWidth = initialWidth + dx;                    newHeight = initialHeight + dy;                } else if (activeHandle.classList.contains('bottom-left')) {                    newWidth = initialWidth - dx;                    newHeight = initialHeight + dy;                } else if (activeHandle.classList.contains('top-right')) {                    newWidth = initialWidth + dx;                    newHeight = initialHeight - dy;                } else if (activeHandle.classList.contains('top-left')) {                    newWidth = initialWidth - dx;                    newHeight = initialHeight - dy;                }                newspaperOutput.style.width = `${Math.max(300, newWidth)}px`;                newspaperOutput.style.height = `${Math.max(300, newHeight)}px`;            };            const onEnd = () => {                activeHandle = null;                window.removeEventListener('mousemove', onMove);                window.removeEventListener('mouseup', onEnd);                window.removeEventListener('touchmove', onMove);                window.removeEventListener('touchend', onEnd);            };            resizeHandles.forEach(handle => {                handle.addEventListener('mousedown', onStart);                handle.addEventListener('touchstart', onStart);            });        });    </script></body></html></div><div class="clearfix"></div></div><div id="custom_html-8" class="widget_text container-wrapper widget widget_custom_html"><div class="textwidget custom-html-widget"><script async type="application/javascript"        src="https://news.google.com/swg/js/v1/swg-basic.js"></script><script>  (self.SWG_BASIC = self.SWG_BASIC || []).push( basicSubscriptions => {    basicSubscriptions.init({      type: "NewsArticle",      isPartOfType: ["Product"],      isPartOfProductId: "CAow76eNCw:openaccess",      clientOptions: { theme: "light", lang: "mr" },    });  });</script></div><div class="clearfix"></div></div></div></aside></div></div></div></div><style>#tiepost-7109-section-9047 .full-overlay-title li:not(.no-post-thumb) .block-title-overlay{background-color: #f8f8f8;}#tiepost-7109-section-9047 .full-overlay-title li:not(.no-post-thumb) .block-title-overlay .post-meta,#tiepost-7109-section-9047 .full-overlay-title li:not(.no-post-thumb) .block-title-overlay a:not(:hover){color: #000000;}#tiepost-7109-section-9047 .full-overlay-title li:not(.no-post-thumb) .block-title-overlay .post-meta{opacity: 0.80;}</style><div id="tiepost-7109-section-9047" class="section-wrapper container-full has-background has-title"><div class="section-item full-width" style="background-color: #f8f8f8;
